# Comments for Question 2, LLM=Claude 3.5 Haiku

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=5.8)
    The plot has a clear arc with the knight's decision-making process forming the narrative spine, but suffers from vagueness about the actual secret and stakes involved. The story achieves a sense of resolution when Aldric decides to release the prisoner, though the consequences remain nebulous. The pacing is uneven—too much time spent on atmospheric description and not enough on concrete plot development. The "seemingly random items" concept is introduced but not fully integrated into the plot mechanics.

  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=5.8)
    The plot follows a logical progression from discovery to revelation, with the seashell effectively driving the action. However, the story lacks a true resolution—we're told Elena is "about to change everything" but never see the consequences. The narrative builds tension well but leaves too many threads dangling. The pacing feels rushed in the final third, with major revelations coming too quickly without sufficient development.

While there's a satisfying thematic arc about cultural preservation, the actual narrative progression feels minimal. The story establishes a situation rather than developing a complete narrative with meaningful change or resolution.
